name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Guestroom (Double bed)
info:Stayed in January 2024
info:Other
info:6 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted January 4, 2024
msg:Bo Yin Hotel (Li River Secluded Hotel)
Our visit to Guilin was to spend time with my wife‚Äôs large family and we twice stayed at the Li River Secluded hotel, for a total of 7 nights. Our expectations of a hotel experience are high, so we avoid using American chain hotels when possible. The Li River Secluded hotel more than met those expectations by combining exceptional customer service with a laid back, but luxurious guest experience. On arrival, we were offered a room upgrade. The upgrade accommodation was located on the ground floor, so this did not appeal to us until we were shown the room ‚Ä¶ the suite was spacious and tastefully furnished with a Zen motif that included a ceremonial tea table. Both my wife and I practice daily yoga, so the ample floor space immediately appealed to us. A room-width picture window featured a view of the Li River Lake and its pair of pagodas. Remote-controlled drapes and shears sound-proofed and eliminated light from the room when closed.
 
A buffet daily breakfast on the 8th (top) floor was included and featured a good selection of both Chinese and Western options. We had family commitments that prevented us from eating dinner at the restaurant, but my wife hosted an afternoon tea session in the restaurant for some of her friends and the tea and pastries were excellent. In addition, fresh fruit was placed in the room every day, and the room refrigerator was refreshed daily with water, sodas, and snacks.
 
The hotel was generally maintained in pristine condition and effected the highest standards of cleanliness. This applied to all the facilities apart from a small exercise room on the 5th floor. This consisted of a set of barbells (no bench), a fixed weight station (functional), and 2 treadmills, neither of which functioned properly ‚Ä¶ that said, I did use the weight station and the patio outside of the exercise room for yoga on a couple warmer days. There was also a guest laundry on the 5th floor which my wife used on one occasion.
 
The customer service attitude in Chinese hotels is generally an improvement on what we are accustomed to in North America, but at the Bo Yin Hotel it‚Äôs exceptional. This means that English language speakers (I‚Äôm Canadian and my wife is Chinese by birth) would experience no problem in addressing any of the front desk, maid, or restaurant personnel. For those who prefer to order take-out food, a robotic delivery service is used, a feature that tends to fascinate any child you might be traveling with.
Sean Bennett

name:Z‚Äço‚Äçe‚Äçy‚Äçx‚Äçi‚Äçy‚Äçi‚Äçx‚Äçi
info:Suite - Night View (Balcony)
info:Stayed in April 2024

info:3 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted April 24, 2024
msg:Live in a brilliant place and have a peaceful vacation in the sound of oars and lights

Speaking of Guilin's cultural landmarks, the Sun and Moon Towers are well-deserved

The golden Sun Tower, 41 meters high, is the tallest existing copper tower in the world

The silver Moon Tower, 35 meters high, is a unique seven-story glazed tower

The two towers shine together, facing each other from afar, forming a unique picture with the lake, curved bridges and woods

At the same time, the two towers form a "easy" character

When planning this trip to Guilin, I will take a good look at this Feng Shui building complex as a goal

So when choosing a hotel, I compared it many times and chose the [Lijiang Boyin Hotel] with the best viewing position

But I was still surprised when I checked in. I knew it was close to the scenic spot, but I didn't expect to go downstairs directly to the scenic spot

You can see the Sun and Moon Towers from different angles in the room, lounge, restaurant and terrace

Walk three Minutes, key scenic spots [Jingjiang Palace, East and West Lane, Zhengyang Pedestrian Street] are all directly accessible 
I accidentally lived in the most golden location in this city 
I sincerely give you a suggestion, don't take a taxi if you live in this location 
It is likely that it will take longer to take a taxi than to walk for 3-5 minutes 

In addition, the hotel is equipped with very complete facilities, and the room environment is high-end. 
The gym, laundry room, restaurant, Starlight Lounge, SPA trea**ent and other supporting specifications are very good 
The Starlight Lounge and restaurant are the most pleasant night view viewing places in the city 
The sun and the moon shine together in the leisurely and close museum; the beautiful scenery in the painting that responds to the mountains and rivers 

In addition, I have to say that the richness of breakfast is really a shot of heart after the rampage scenic spots

msg:The experience of staying in the Lijiang River for one night is the feeling of [dream], yes, it is such an unreal word. When I was lying on the sofa on the balcony, facing the wind blowing from the Sun and Moon Twin Pagodas and Shanhu Lake, I remembered what Chen Yi said: I would like to be a Guilin native, not a fairy. At this moment I feel like a fairy.
Lijiang Poyin should be the facade of the Poyin Hotel Group. It opened on May 1, 2018. The facilities in the room are very well maintained. Only when you use the non-smart toilet in the bathroom, do you realize that this is a hotel that has been in business for four years. Tables, chairs, carpets, bedding are all new, and there is a JBL Horizon at the head of the bed, and the sound quality is excellent. Kohler sanitary ware and APPELLES accessories are all standard in the Boyin room. The mattress should be made of latex, soft and supportive, and the hot water in the bathroom should not be too hot. The sincerity is reflected in these details. It should have cost a lot of money when it was built.
Even in the best location between the central square and Rongshan Lake, the room size is still very large, and it will not feel compact at all. Looking out from the balcony is full of greenery, and there is also a tea room in the room. Here, drinking tea and listening to the rain, I really feel that I am living a fairy-like life. Don't miss the Galaxy Lounge and Yunyun Restaurant on the roof. The scenery is good and the decoration is very tasteful. Friends also praised the cakes produced by its afternoon tea with good ingredients, which are better than many Internet celebrity cake shops.
Even if the hotel is in the best location between the central square and Rongshan Lake, the room size is still large, and it will not feel compact at all. The service of the hotel really makes me feel that I have done my best to the second time. When I checked in, the clerk warmly led me to the elevator entrance. During the period, there was welcome fruit, the bath was equipped with a bathtub cover, and there were disinfectant wipes beside the toilet. Nongfu Spring is available in the customer service aisle for self-pickup. The platform on the fifth floor is also equipped with a swimming pool, a gym and a sauna. With the view of the twin towers, it is really invincible, and it has fully achieved the hardware level that a five-star should have. Special thanks to Damei and Axin for their service~ Thank you Lijiang Boyin for giving me such an unforgettable stay experience!

msg:Due to the epidemic and the nature of my wife's work place, I can't travel far, but the children at home are clamoring to go out to play every day. ~ Just had the opportunity to stay at the Lijiang Boyin Hotel in Guilin, the overall feeling is still very good, it is worth recommending.
    First of all, in terms of geographical location, the hotel is located in Yangqiaotou, Zhongshan South Road, Guilin City, a proper downtown area of the old city of Guilin City, and is located on the edge of the urban area with two rivers and four lakes. The transportation is very convenient and the surrounding scenery is pleasant. At the same time, there are also the Zhengyang Road Pedestrian Street in Guilin City, the Central Square, the new landmarks of Dongxi Lane and Xiaoyao Building in the urban area of Guilin City (these are all in the center for the Spring Festival Gala). It is very good to walk around in the evening.
    The hotel room is neat, clean and well equipped. We stayed in a parent-child room. For the children in the house, we arranged a separate one-piece wooden bed. The bathroom adopts the method of separating the shower room and toilet into two areas. This is a great point, especially for those of us who bring children to play. Family, this is very important~! (Otherwise it would be embarrassing...) The balcony is equipped with a chaise longue sofa and a coffee table for drinking tea. At the same time, it is equipped with a toy, a small room and a tent that children can play with. The second child likes it very much. The tea bar is equipped with a coffee machine and capsules, which is very convenient. Just in time for me to work overtime at night, the coffee is just right!
    There is a children's playground on the first floor of the hotel. Due to the epidemic, there are no people in the bar, and the two children are very happy. There is a swimming pool and gym on the fifth floor, which is very good, but because the weather is not very suitable, I didn't go swimming. There is a cloud restaurant on the roof, which is very good. You can see a beautiful night view of the two rivers and four lakes.
    The breakfast is delivered to the room, if it is not enough, you can order more. The experience is very good, the service is warm and thoughtful, and it is worthwhile for tourists who want to stay in the city center~! Worth recommending~!
    Finally, I hope that the epidemic will end soon, and everyone will return to normal work and life~! You can travel anywhere~!

There is a welcome porridge on arrival the night of the first day.

The only shortcoming is Wi-Fi, the bandwidth is insufficient, sometimes it will be out of power, including the connection method can also be more formal, I hope it can be improved.
